10/05/2021, 21:56 - Suvrodeep Jsr: *Greetings to all the valiant and mettlesome gamers!*

Drumroll Please! 
Here we are for the first-ever gaming tournament of NIT, Jamshedpur *Survival Battlefield*, a Call of Duty(COD) mobile tournament.
So, all the game enthusiasts assemble and gear up.

The tournament is open for the whole first year and all the league matches will be held between *13th-15th of May 2021*.

There are two ways to participate:

1. You can participate in a team 5. Only one member from each team(leader) will fill the google doc form given below. Make sure all the team members are from NIT, Jamshedpur as no inter-college teams are allowed.

https://forms.gle/v3mTefwQEF5eKEto8


2. You can participate individually also, just fill the google form below and we will assign you a team.

https://forms.gle/wCmVBjDQsc4Fdo6Y9

*Some Important rules and guidelines:*

1. You are not allowed to use
    i) Banned items Akimbo & NA 45
    ii) Ballistic Shield & Transform Shield
    iii) Emulators

2. No third-party software is allowed.

3. Only mobile devices must be used.

4. All cheat/hack/glitches/exploitation of bugs are strictly prohibited.

5. The map of the game will be selected by the team winning the toss.

6. Participants must be from the first year only.

7. There will be a set of 3 games between each pair of teams ( Team Deathmatch, Domination, Search & Destroy).

9. All the final decisions will be taken by the organizers

19/05/2021, 15:45 - +91 95481 12742: Hey everyone,
I hope all of you are safe and doing fine, please take care of yourself and your family. That's the most important thing at the moment. 

Yesterday Ojass announced its three-day festival from 21st of this month named *Case Fiesta, NIT Jamshedpur's first and only festival dedicated to the art of problem-solving and case studies.* Looking at the participation count I thought that maybe you guys don't have a clear idea about what case studies are and it's importance, *so I thought that maybe I could help you guys out with some necessary info.* 

 *What are case studies* - Corporate problems inspired by real-life business situations. You'll get a situation and numerous sets of data. Analyzing the data given you need to answer some questions both analytical and qualitative. For eg. An international chain looking for expansion opportunities in India, you need to answer questions like expected market share, profit, revenue, etc based on the data provided. 

 *Why case studies -* Most important question but I'll answer this with one word and I'll repeat it three times just for the sake of its importance - *Placements! Placements! and Placements! Why, here is the reason -* 
1) More than 70% of the companies in the non-core sector that are not branch specific either venture in the domain of data analytics, data science, consultancy, or finance. 
2) And almost all of these companies have a separate case study round to check the problem-solving ability of the applicant. 
3) Consultancy and Finance giants *like ZS Associates, EXL, etc organize case study competitions namely ZS Campus Beats and EXL EQ* . *Winners are directly offered PPO ( Pre - Placement Offer) which means you get placed even without entering the placement season.* 

I know you guys have exams but trust me this is equally important if not more. We never got an opportunity like this in our first years, if I had this opportunity in my freshman year I would have grabbed it with both my hands. That's why I really want you guys to capitalize on this opportunity. Don't let it go guys. 

As CR's I hope you will be able to motivate your classmates to participate. Try explaining it to them in your unofficial groups. Sorry for the long message 😅😅. 
Cheers

28/06/2021, 14:52 - Shiv Cse: _Some doubts regarding making notes for MF and sir's response to that_ ==>>
1. Sir jitna ppt me diya gaya hai bas utna hi likhna hai, ya kuch additional bhi likhna hoga?
2. Kya A4 size sheet me notes bana sakte hai?
3. If I am making notes for say "foundry shop", then how long should be in terms of no. of pages?
4. Should the notes contain all the diagrams which are given in ppt?
5. In our last shop ie Carpentry shop, there is one practical at the end of the ppt (containing aim, tools required, procedure etc.). Should we write that also in addition to its respective notes?

6. What details should we give on 1st page like name, subject, index??

7. Sir, there are multiple experiment/practicals for each chapters/lab found in internet. How many and which ones to prepare?? 

8. Anything you would like to add.. 

 _Sir's Response==>_ 
1. The pdf file should contain 4 chapters (of each 4 labs). Each chapter will have 2 sections: i. Theory, ii. Practical. Theory you can gather from any source (from ppt shown in class, or any book or internet source). In case of book or internet source, you have to mention from which source you have taken the information. In Practical section, you have to write Aim, Tools used and procedure and safety precautions.

2. Yes, theory notes plus practical both in A4 sheets.

3. There is not limit on number of pages.

4. Not all, but as much as possible. Mostly of the tools that were used.

5. See pt. 1.

6. First page: Name, Roll No., Dept, Subject. Second Page: Table of Contents with page number.Third page onwards reports

7. One experiment each lab.

8. Anything else you want to ask? 

(So if you want to ask any doubt regarding ```MF notes making``` make sure that that the question should differ from the one mentioned above)

28/06/2021, 15:50 - Ujjwal Nitjsr: This delightful play on English words was too good to keep to myself ....*

*How every English letter can be (annoyingly) silent.*

English is maddening, and it's not sorry. English can be such an intractable heel, especially when it comes to its spelling: for every rule explaining how a letter is pronounced in a given situation it often seems like there is a herd of exceptions mooing about how the rule doesn't apply. Letters persist in words despite not playing any discernible role in the word's pronunciation. It's maddening for those of us who are peeved by such things.

A
The a in bread (as well as in tread) does nothing. You might as well spell it bred except that then it looks too much like the past tense of breed. So don't do that.

B
Most silent b's come at the ends of words and just after m: bomb, climb, comb, crumb, dumb, lamb, limb, numb, plumb, thumb, tomb. Just when one starts to feel comfortable with the relative regularity of these, debt and subtle show up like a couple of toughs.

C
C may as well cede all power to s in words like science and scissors, but we'll also point out that it's not doing much of anything in acquire, indict, or muscle.

D
D is shirking its auditory duties in handkerchief and mostly doing the same in handsome. Its appearance in Wednesday can only be seen as some kind of cruel joke.

E
The word sleeve has an excessive number of e's. We're saying it right now. Sleve or sleev would work fine, but English does not like to leave v's on the ends of words; it props them up with e's, as though they'd fall over otherwise. That v habit explains, then, words like leave and give, but there's no excusing the e in words like imagine.

F
While some people do in fact pronounce the second f in fifth, the first pronunciation given in our dictionary is the one that omits it. Overall, however, f is to be commended for its performance generally. We'd give it an A, if we were on speaking terms with that letter.

G
G has no business being in sign nor phlegm, as far as the modern reader is concerned. It obviously doesn't care. This callousness is also evident in that slew of gn- words: gnarl, gnash, gnat, gnaw, gnostic, gnu. It can be no surprise, then, that g also participates in the likes of such offenses as high, though, and through.

H
The h's at the beginning of heir, honest, and honor have nothing to say. Neither do the ones in rhyme and ghost. That h makes a contribution of a sort in the second syllable of rhythm only goes so far in repairing the letter's record.

I
I doesn't do a blessed thing in business, except to be impersonated by the u in the first syllable. It also does no discernible good in suit, which in a decent orthographic system would be spelled soot.

J
Some of you may be happy to know that we have at this point only one English word in which the j is silent: marijuana.

K
The silent k in a slew of common words demonstrates a callousness for beginner spellers especially: knee, knife, knight, knit, knob, knock, knot, know, knuckle.

L
The most indecent of the silent l words is surely colonel. The word sounds identical to kernel, which is an honorable, respectfully spelled word. L is also silent in could, should, would, as well as in calf and half, and in chalk, talk, walk, and for many people in calm, palm, and psalm.

M
One can get through much of life never encountering m in its silent form. By the time a person is ready for a word like mnemonic they have likely come to accept the vagaries of silent letters.

N
Like silent b's, silent n's tend to come at the ends of words and after m: autumn, column, damn, hymn, limn, solemn. While this might suggest to some that m is a little too accommodating, we would never anthropomorphize letters in such a way.

O
There is the flagrant excess of letters in enough, rough, and tough, where o is among several who have no place being there. Then there is the formerly mentioned ruffian colonel, in which neither o behaves properly and the second o doesn't even bother to try. But in addition to those we then also have jeopardy, leopard, and people. We'll let you draw your own conclusions about o.

P
P is silent before n in a selection of somewhat technical terms, such as pneumonia and pneumatic. And it's silent before s in a different selection of words such as psalm, psyche, and psychology. It boldly says nothing in corps and coup and receipt. In some pronunciations of comptroller it somehow convinces m to join with it in dissembling; the two there impersonate n.

Q
Q tends to function wholly aboveboard as an upstanding member of the alphabet. Most of us are fortunate to encounter its dereliction in lacquer only occasionally.

R
R exists in forecastle only to mock landlubbers. It exists in February only to make us suffer.

S
S is a mostly-reliable letter. Its failings are limited largely to aisle, apropos, debris, isle, and island. We cannot, however, overlook its participation in the hot mess that is bourgeois.

T
T refuses to be audible in ballet, castle, listen, and whistle. In asthma it conspires with h to shun its usual duties.

U
U may appear reasonable, but evidence to the contrary is not difficult to find: build, catalogue, dialogue, colleague, guard, guess, laugh, league, tongue. Note that the second and third of these words have attempted eviction and are meeting with significant success: catalog and dialog are both fully accepted variant spellings.

V
V is at this point the only letter that refuses to be unheard in any established word of the language. And yet a dark cloud gathers on the horizon: in late May 2017 a much-followed and likely sleep-addled Twitter user tweeted out what was clearly a partially developed composition. The Internet seized on the enigmatic final word and discussed it ad nauseam. Of the myriad pronunciations suggested for this non-word, several of the strongest contenders had a silent v.

W
W yields all power to the r that follows it in wrack, wraith, wrangle, wrap, wreath, wren, wrench, wrestle, wrinkle, wrist, writ, write, wrong, and wrought. As if that lot were not enough, w with no apparent logic whatsoever sits idly silent in answer, sword, two, and who as well.

X
We will admit to some small appreciation of x's discretion in its orthographic indiscretion. Its silence seems perhaps calculated in faux and faux pas.

Y
We cannot blame y for its gratuitous presence in beyond. The letter may, in fact, believe itself to be essential in the word. It cannot be ignored, however, that the word would reasonably have its same pronunciation if it were spelled "beond," "beeond," or "be-ond."

Z
There will surely be attempts to blame the French, and yet the following have been fully established members of the English language for centuries now: chez, laissez-faire, and rendezvous. We cannot look the other way, Z.

27/07/2021, 15:40 - Suvrodeep Jsr: Sir,
This mail highlights the prime issues faced by the students in online semester and the urgent need for calling us back to campus.

Sir due to online teaching and current scenario there's now a confusion among the students that will they ever be able to attend college offline or not?

Many of us have already taken the first dose of vaccine and there are also some who are completely vaccinated.

I would like to urge you to please plan a complete procedure and protocols so that we can be safely accomodated into college. I'll like to put forth example of AIIMS which have called their students for offline classes and are taking enough care of their health by asking vaccination reports, RT-PCR test reports etc. Why can't these be implemented in our college sir? 


We are tired by false hopes. The dream of studying inside college campus seems blurred now. With every passing semester, we expect a notice of college reopening, but all your notices are limited to fee payment. I really don't think the education we're being given in this online mode is worth Rs. 77,500. The core ideas of engineering are missing, which may further hamper our placements and that's itself a nightmare. 

I, therefore hope that you understand our concern and reply in positive sense. Our only demand is re-opening the college, something which you must think about. 

Thank You.

*HOW TO REGISTER ?*

*FOR THOSE WHO PAID THEIR FEE THROUGH QFIX*

Login to MIS website using this *link*
👉 14.139.205.166/NITJ

Upload the required documents
1) fee receipt (current semester /sem 3)
2) grade card (last semester/sem 2)
3) Last income certificate (For now, upload that IC which you had uploaded in the fee remission form) *Point 3) is only for students availing some sort of remission*

*FEE DETAILS*

1)Tuition fee receipt no = Qfix reference no 
2)Total amount = actual amount before decimal point (eg; 15075)
3)tuition fee date = fee payment date 

4)mees fee receipt no = XXXXX
5)mess fee amount = 0
6)mess fee date = same as tuition fee date 

7)fine fee receipt no= XXXXX
8)fine fee amount = 0 
9)fine fee date = same as tuition fee date

01/10/2021, 17:38 - +91 8340 331 709: Hello 2k20!

With the numerous clubs into your picture, *Team Innoreva* is the official IOT, ML/DL team of NITJSR. At a budding age, we encourage and help innovative minds in the field of Internet of things(IOT), Machine Learning, embedded systems,etc. We also provide the much needed industry exposure to the students.
One of the up and coming technologies to power the digital transformation of industries across the globe brought forth by industry 4.0 is, of course, the IoT. 

IoT describes the network of physical objects—“things”—that are embedded with sensors, software, and other technologies for the purpose of connecting and exchanging data with other devices and systems over the internet.
One cannot imagine that the number of IoT devices today have officially surpassed the amount of humans in the world. 

So, let's dive into the world of automation where we assure everything you want to know and get started with. Gear up for the incoming session!!

 *Regarding Sever Issues* 

There had been some server issues in last three examinations. Attempts have been made to rectify the problem and solve the issue, the server will be under continuous surveillance of the web team and they will try that no such problem arises in future.

However if any issue comes up during upload then emails are accepted within the designated time window. This is to specifically inform that the 2 hour 15 minute time window is divided in the following manner - 2 hours for completing the paper and 15 minutes for uploading your answersheet. Please adhere to the time limit and do not utilize uploading time in writing.

 In case any server issue comes up then emails within the designated time window ( before 12:45 PM) will be accepted by the faculty, the faculty can confirm the same directly from academics. But decision regarding any email sent after 12:45 PM shall solely reside with the faculty. So if you are emailing then please try to send it before the deadline and utilize the fifteen minutes window for uploading purpose only.

Hacktoberfest is a yearly event to encourage people to contribute to open source in October. It’s a celebration of community, learning and giving back. Go ahead and fill out the Contributors Submissions form. Make one successful pull request in October. 
The programming club of NIT Jamshedpur, PCON is back with it’s yearly event, Hacktoberfest. Think about projects you already use and benefit from, or search through your own project’s dependencies. Hacktoberfest can be an especially welcoming time to contribute to projects that are new to you. The official website of hacktoberfest is here: https://hacktoberfest.digitalocean.com/
Hacktoberfest can be an especially welcoming time to dip your toes into open source contributions for the first time. There’s plenty of streams, posts, guides, and conversations around getting started. You’re joining many folks also starting their journey this month!
The Github link is here where you can contribute: https://github.com/pcon-hacktoberfest-21

Greetings from NIT Jamshedpur, 
The Monty Quiz was born two years ago at NIT Jamshedpur, in the loving memory of one of our finest alumni, Late Flight Lieutenant Sunit Mohanty, who was martyred when his AN-32 aircraft crashed near the Pari Hills on June 3rd, 2019. He was a true gentleman in every sense and one of the best quizzers of NIT Jamshedpur.

The first and second editions of this quiz saw huge participation from across the country. And now we are back with the third! 

Monty Quiz 3.0 will take place on 7th Nov, 2021 - the birth anniversary of our hero. And it will be hosted by none other than Major Chandrakant Nair, but before that, we will be proceeding with the Prelims Round 1 for the quiz on the 31st Oct, 2021 on D2C. Due to the pandemic, like the previous year, the quiz will be held virtually this year also.

And what will you play for? Well apart from the glory of becoming part of this quiz, the total prize money of INR 75K is at stake, where the winning team takes INR 30K, runner up INR 18K, the second runner up wins a sum of INR 12K and each finalist team also gets a cash prize of INR 2K.

Whether you are an expert or just a curious person, we assure you that it'll be a great experience. So don't miss this chance to compete with the best quizzers in the country and win exciting prizes. 

For any queries, contact:
Trisurya - 7044224104
Anirban - 9693947512

22/10/2021, 20:36 - Suvrodeep Jsr: *NOTICE* 

 *REGARDING THE REOPENING OF THE INSTITUTE* 

Dear Friends,

There were a lot of speculations and assumptions floating around the reopening of our institute so I request all my fellow colleagues to please carefully read this notice from top to bottom. I hope all the doubts and apprehensions will get cleared after this.

 *The Students' Council of NIT Jamshedpur had the final meeting with the agenda of " Reopening the institute in a phase-wise manner " with the administration on 22nd October 2021(i.e today) at 4:00 P.M.* The meeting was chaired and attended by Hon'ble Director Sir, all the members of The Dean Panel, all Head of Departments, The Chief Warden, and other office-bearers. Members of the council presented their opinions on the subject and made our stand very clear on the matter. We presented the idea of phase-wise opening from next semester while classes and examinations remain in online mode. However there were some apprehensions which were put forth by some HOD's and The Chief Warden, particularly in relation to less number of doubly vaccinated students in the final year ( 56% to be precise as per the survey we conducted on 27th September 2021 ) and regarding the end semester examinations, most of the faculty members suggested reopening from next semester. However, after some deliberation, we were given two choices by Hon'ble Director Sir-

 *1st - We report on 15th November, stay quarantined for five days, and then give End Semester Examination in offline mode. (i.e. in the institute on paper with invigilation)* 

 *2nd- We give our End Semester Examination in online mode from our homes ( tentatively in the last week of November or first week of December) and then report immediately after that to the institute probably in December itself.* 

Members of The Studnets' Council strongly felt that since classes had been held in the online medium for the entire semester most of us will not be able to shift to offline examination mode suddenly, and it would also cause difficulty for students who will not be able to come back to the campus. We were also clear on the stand that under no condition shall results or examinations of students be hampered. Hence The Students' Council in unanimity decided to go with the second option. 

Hence the decision regarding the reopening of the institute, for now, is as follows-

 *" All Final Year and Pre-Final Year students will give their End Semester Examinations from their homes in online medium only. After the examinations end both the 2K18 and 2K19 batch will be called to the campus in a phase-wise manner. For the 2K20 batch classes will continue in the online medium, for now, they will be called back to the campus next semester as and when the conditions will be favourable.* 

Also for all those students who will return to the campus *DOUBLE DOSAGE OF VACCINATION and A NEGATIVE RTPCR ( NOT MORE THAN 72 HOURS OLD ) WILL BE MANDATORY."* 

 *Hence it is my humble appeal especially to all the Final Year and Pre-Final Year students that they complete both their doses as soon as possible. It is mandatory and also in the best interest of everyone.* 

I have tried to present everything that underwent in the meeting and the reopening process as a whole with utmost transparency in front of all the students. I as the President of the Students' Council take full responsibility for the choice and decision that we made. We felt that under the given circumstances this was in the best interest of every student. If anyone has any doubt regarding the decision or wants to raise any issue in this regard then please feel free to contact me anytime 24*7. 

Once again I would like to stress my appeal to all the students that please take both doses of vaccination before December 2021. It will be a mandatory requirement if you want to return to the campus. From now on we will collect weekly data on vaccination and the reports will be duly sent to the administration. 

I know that many of us especially my final year colleagues were expecting the institute to reopen by November 2021. I extend my apologies to all my friends who may have felt disappointed with this decision. I would also thank all my fellow batchmates who gave in their valuable inputs at regular intervals. Once again I apologize personally if anyone felt let down.

With that being said I promise that we will continue to take follow-ups on further developments in this regard. It would mean the world to me if all of us can be back on the campus and everything returns to being normal. 

Thank You for the love and support. Until next time...  

--
Regards,
Mayank Kumar
President, Students' Council
National Institute of Technology Jamshedpur
Email: president.sc@nitjsr.ac.in
Phone: 9075167388

24/11/2021, 12:30 - Ujjwal Nitjsr: Guideline for online exam.

1. This is an open book exam. You can use books, notes, or other study material. Discussing with each other, taking human help, and searching on the internet is not allowed.
2. Student particulars, especially name and roll number on the answer notebook should be written properly. Violating it will result in 5 marks deduction. 
3. You can solve questions in order of your preference. However, while scanning keep the question order preferably the same as given in the question paper.
Don't scan a part of the answer which you don't want to be checked. (Crop your scanning accordingly)
4. All subparts of a question should be done together in one place. 
5. Scan with a good scanner which makes the background white. Try to keep the file size minimum. Use a scanner app which doesn't leave any watermark or its stamp.
6. Use a calculator.
7. Keep an alternate internet connection handy preferably from a different service provider. Submit your answer books well before time.
A grace period of 15 minutes is given only to handle casualties such as slow internet connection. This period should not be used for writing or scanning.

How do we detect copies answers
8. You have made a mistake somewhere that mistake should be carried forwarded throughout the answer.
9. Similarly, if you have derived a formula then your numerical answer (if applicable) should match with it.
10. If an answer of a question given in an unusual manner by several students then it is suspected as copied answer.

10/01/2022, 22:20 - +91 8340 331 709: *NOTICE ( for issues regarding fee remission)* 

 (Please refer to the notice rolled out by the academic section on 29th October 2021 for info regarding the remission process and deadlines issued. You'll find this in your groups.)


Looking at the recent issues that students are facing regarding fee remission and payment portal, we are rolling out following clarifications-

 *1) For those who had submitted correct documents on time and within the deadline mentioned in the notice and yet the payment portal is showing the wrong amount -* 

For all such students, the associate dean has assured us that he will cross check the lists and if any such cases are found then the payment portal will be updated accordingly. All such students shall not face any problem. 

 *2) Students who submitted their documents late /in wrong format /did not submit / missed some documents / similar issues -* 

For all such students the amount on the portal has been updated as the documents were not verified due to the above mentioned reasons. We have requested for an extension window for all such students so that they can resubmit their correct documents. We are in dialogue with the academics for the same. We cannot garuntee or promise anything, however if any extension is granted an official notice will be circulated regarding the same, in such a case extra fee will be remitted to your accounts later. However, as of now all such students are requested to pay the fee that is being shown on the portal. 

Once again I reiterate that the decision regarding extension window lies solely with the academics, we have put forth our points but nothing can be promised.

Also the qfix portal is active hence all the students who don't have any doubts can now pay their fees.

For doubts, please feel free to contact any of the members or write an email at president.sc@nitjsr.ac.in.

Regards,
The Students' Council of NIT Jamshedpur
